Xiǎo Míng jué de shùxuékè hěn kūzào，suǒyǐ yí shàng shùxuékè jiù fànkùn。
Xiao Ming finds the math class boring and feels sleepy whenever he has one.
这地方太干燥，皮肤总觉得干巴。
Zhè dìfāng tài gānzào，pífū zǒng juédé gànba。
It is dry in this area, my skin is always dry here.
他建议我平时把数码相机放在干燥箱里。
Tā jiànyì wǒ píngshí bǎ shùmǎ xiàng jī fàngzài gānzàoxiāng lǐ。
He advised me to put the digital camera in a dry cabinet when I am not using it.
这个专题片虽然有意义，但可视性不强，挺枯燥。
Zhège zhuāntípiān suīrán yǒu yìyì，dàn kěshìxìng bùqiáng，tǐng kūzào。
Although this monographic film is meaningful, it isn\'t fun to watch and is very boring.
一个月没下雨，天气太干燥了，家里只好靠空气加湿器来调节湿度了。
Yígè yuè méi xiàyǔ，tiānqì tài gānzào le，jiā lǐ zhǐhǎo kào kōngqì jiāshīqì lái tiáojié shīdù le。
It hasn\'t rained for one month. It is so dry in the room that we have to use a humidifier.
走了这么远的路一口水都没有喝，我被弄得口干舌燥。
Zǒu le zhème yuǎn de lù yìkǒu shuǐ dōu méiyǒu hē，wǒ bèi nòng de kǒugān shézào。
Having had no water after such a long walk, I am extremely thirsty.
在开着暖风机的房间里呆久了，她觉得皮肤有些干燥。
Zài kāi zhe nuǎnfēngjī de fángjiān lǐ dāi jiǔ le，tā juédé pífū yǒuxiē gānzào。
Being in the room with a convection heater on, she felt her skin was a little bit dry.
干燥的柴禾在火堆里噼啪作响。
Gānzào de cháihé zài huǒduī lǐ pīpā zuòxiǎng。
The dry faggots crackled in the fire.
在干燥的季节里，我每天都要抹一些润肤膏。
Zài gānzào de jìjié lǐ，wǒ měitiān dōuyào mǒ yìxiē rùnfūgāo。
In dry seasons, I would apply some moisture cream every day.
一般来说，吸水性强的物质均可用作干燥剂。
Yìbān láishuō，xīshuǐxìng qiáng de wùzhì jūnkě yòngzuò gānzàojì。
Generally speaking, water-absorbing materials can all be used as a desiccant.
冬天风干物燥，必须小心管理香火，否则易引发火灾。
Dōngtiān fēnggān wùzào，bìxū xiǎoxīn guǎnlǐ xiānghuǒ，fǒuzé yì yǐnfā huǒzāi。
It is dry in winter, you must take charge of the burning joss sticks and watch out for fire.
由于天气太干燥，家具木板都绽开了。
Yóuyú tiānqì tài gānzào，jiājù mùbǎn dōu zhànkāi le。
Due to the extremely dry weather, the furniture boards all burst open.
这些货物怕潮，储存的时候别忘了放干燥剂。
Zhèxiē huòwù pà cháo，chǔcún de shíhou bié wàng le fàng gānzàojì。
These goods are susceptible to water, remember to add a desiccant when you store them.

We just had nothing in common and I couldn\'t communicate with his dull friends.

I hate painting it is so slow and boring.

My sweater is now bone dry.

我的毛衣现在十分干燥。

组织胞浆菌病是由蝙蝠和鸟类传播的疾病。

水族馆里的混浊水质是由细菌繁殖引起的，而绿色的水是由藻类繁殖引起的。

肠道内的细菌消耗食物中的维生素B12。

这种昆虫能携带并传播一些危险的细菌。
